< review>
Super fun experience, good selection of drinks, and we really enjoyed the available lawn games after we got off the train.
Only reason for 4 stars is that the train just moves in a straight line forward, stops for a while to ensure you get your full time, then moves back along the same line. Would've been cool to have a loop.</review>

<time>1604454606718<//time><Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
I lucked out and ended up going twice, one week in-between visits. The weather was incredible, and I would recommend paying close attention to the forecast when you book your visit. They did a nice job communicating tips prior to arrival. However, please note if you are taking elderly folks, there is some walking on uneven ground/gravel required. As well as a hill. Also, getting into the bikeseat requires a little agility and balance.
We managed and it was a lovely trip, both times. You can get away with very little pedaling if you choose. The fellas who run the ride are patient and informative - consider  tipping in the tip jar after the ride!
Both trips (October 2020) offered complimentary bottles of water or Gatorade and hand sanitizer was available on the picnic tables. Please note there are outhouses for use and a washing station for hands but no indoor plumbing if that is a requirement of yours. The trip time was true to expected schedule, there is a basket to bungee your pack if you bring one, water bottle holders and the seats have rain holes should you ride in a shower. They run rain or shine.<//text>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
Fun train ride, especially if you like themed rides. This was the Great Train Robbery, complete with "money" that the bandit on board takes during the hold up. The stop for lunch was good, though hot out (is about summer here). BBQ served. If vegan or vegetarian, will need to find out if food for diet is available ahead of time. Relaxing, slower  (approx.10 mph) ride through farm land and river area.</review>

<pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMxx60eHifPbGN-9pwVv4KqcpXNzXMUWcFt89Od=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNFqd1hhgMuvA4z-QIy6nqOnbM605SHsYPCs7cs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNHpVZQ4MLyiKRGzvA1urNYiyF0NrXe73iOrw5r=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMdzF2vnTZNIaOHACnOuzV2pd6OCrBhSa4K0LcQ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNMQdatACNxp9uiu9o1fkd5URu2g3laMK3bI5ai=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><resp>None< /resp><gmapID>0x809ad43a83294c9b:0xaf43fad57d73efda<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<review>We took a ride on the Christmas train yesterday. It was like an unsuccessful purchase from Aliexpress - expectations and reality did not coincide at all. The children and I were placed along the sides of an open car, not a passenger car, with the sides covered with a tarpaulin. The sides do not protect from the cold, because they have huge holes, and you will not be able to look out the window, because this part of the tarpaulin is not transparent. And I wanted to look out the window - because we spent quite a long time just on a trip without any activity from the "elves". Even without music, she wasn't playing at the time. A couple of games played by the elves were not bad, but most of the time we just didn't hear our "elf" because of the noise of the wheels and other noise, and it worked without a microphone. Heating was not carried out by the most stable and reliable structures, one of the two in our car broke down halfway, the second just loomed menacingly over the passengers, swaying when moving. My children and I were put on folding plastic chairs and my youngest daughter fell off it a couple of times. In general, if you are waiting for something like in the photo in the ad - a cozy cute wagon - do not hope. You will be carried like firewood. We also took a couple of smeared photos on the phone with Santa, without even making sure that Santa is visible in the frame. Santa is sitting behind the glass-it is clear that this is the cost of the situation, but it is not heard and he does not hear. As a result, the children said that everything is clear, it is not real. PS Two stars only for the delicious cocoa and the friendliness of most of the staff.<//review>< name>
Olga Klimina</name>

<userid>103367243527770741636<//userid><name>Marjo M< /name><Date>1575079971775< /Date><rating>2<//rating>< Text>
If you were expecting the Polar Express experience for their Christmas Train ride, think again

Pros:
+ Check in process we very smooth and easy
+ Beautiful decorations
+ Love that we were served hot chocolate in appropriate cups with lids and drink stoppers to decrease potential spilling accidents
+ The man with guitar and kazoo and harmonica was a very good musician
+ Snowball fight in the end was extremely fun

Cons:
- It was hard to identify which tables were ours since only one table was labeled! We had 5 adults, 3 children -- It was not clear that we had a 3rd table (2 of 2 seat tables, 1 of 4 seat table), so we were squeezed in to our first 2 tables until someone corrected our seating arrangement.
- We could NOT HEAR the storyteller.. The poor lady was screaming to the top of her lungs and it was just not loud enough.
- The production was extremely sub-par for the price that we paid. I understand that we are technically not at a broadway show, but the script was extremely awkward and disorganized

Other:
* I probably would not recommend this experience to other friends an families, but in case you want to test it out for yourself, I would recommend it for families with kids age 5 or under<//Text>

< Text>
Is it possible to have fun at the dentist? I'm here to tell you it can be. The La Mesa Dental Group is without a doubt, the best dental group I have ever been to. I started going there back in 2009. Since then the office and staff have been reliably helpful, happy, and pleasant...each and every visit!

You can tell when go to a place if people like their job. Are they genuinely happy and eager to help? Or are they frowning and reluctant to acknowledge you? At La Mesa Dental Group, it's all smiles (pun intended). Seriously, it must be a great place to work for because all the staff are so nice!

OK, so here is the best part...Dr. Rob Low. He is a great dentist with a great sense of humor. I'm not sure if he is like this with all his patients, but he has me cracking up all the time. Don't get me wrong, while he is drilling he is professional and all business....but during exams he can be a hoot to listen to.

So yeah, I'm a big fan of this place. I never thought I'd ever be so happy with a dentist. I used to fear the dentist! Going to La Mesa Dental Group makes the pain of a dental visit much more bearable.</Text>

This shop is probably one of the best around.

It will say the location is on Newhall Ranch rd, but the entrance is not. You‚Äôll want to turn onto Avenue Tibbits, and then it will be the first entrance on your left into the large business building)

From driving up right away I knew that the quality of work would be fantastic. They have a large building, with 2 floors and offer a very wide selection of detailing products, wheels, wraps, tints, etc. in their lobby/store.

They have a nice lounge area if you intend on waiting around if you‚Äôre doing a small job, or if you don‚Äôt want to wait around, they will offer you their loaner car for free (just have to provide a credit card for liability) which is a Tesla Model 3. The loaner car made this really nice, even though I was only having my front windows tint matched and it was a short appointment.

Pricing is good too. Not cheap, but not expensive either.  They are very fair. I paid $120 for my front windows to be matched.

I‚Äôll definitely be coming here again. My fianc√©‚Äôs lease is ending very soon, and we‚Äôre going to be getting a new car that will need some nice new shades, and we‚Äôre excited to come back here.< /Text>

<Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
Found Autokinsz a couple of months ago and decided to contact them. I emailed them for some estimates and Jake and Greg responded back in less than a day. I even got responses back from them on non-business hours.

Took my vehicle in just for a Hand Wash and checked out their new location. Shonna and Jake were at the front desk and I filled out a check-in sheet. They asked me if I wanted a loaner car. Really? A loaner car just for a hand wash? That is so awesome! I politely declined the loaner as I told them I would just wait for it.

While I waited, I talked to Shonna about the products they use, about 3M window tint, and got some estimates from her. She explained to me the difference between the FX Premium, Color Stable, and Crystalline films. Just a FYI, the Crystalline film is the top of the line so it'll be more expensive than FX and Color Stable films.

The Hand Wash took longer than anticipated but that was because they were going over the car multiple times to make sure it was clean so this shows they pay attention to detail. Even though my car currently does not have the best paint finish, it looked so much cleaner than going to a fast car wash place. The wheels were very clean with no brake dust on the face of the rim. They even used tire dressing that had a matte finish and not that super glossy finish that can sling all over the side of the rear bumper.

Customer service was spot on which is why I'm giving AutoSkinz 5-Stars on this review. Jake and Shonna were awesome to talk to and answered all my questions and I appreciate their awesome service.<//Text>

< Review>
Cool little bar that came recommended from a bartender @ The Douglass Room - apparently his cousin runs this place. We managed to get seats at a little table by the bar, and someone dropped off a menu. I got Masterstroke ($13), which has rum, umeshu plum liqueur, celery shrub, and gold leaf. I was excited about the gold leaf but it was more like tiny gold dust on the surface of the cocktail lol. Anyways, it was good nonetheless. I like the intimate vibe but I can see how it could easily become overcrowded during prime times.</Review>

< Text>
Oh the beauty that is Ever Bar. This is a review for the Miracle at the Everly pop up Christmas bar!

My friends were super excited to check this place out when we first heard about it.  This place was open on Christmas Day!  The easiest way to park is just to have the hotel valet your car.  Parking is $10 for three hours. This is whether or not you actually do end up staying the entire three hours.

When we first stepped it, which is just a few steps to the left upon entering the hotel, we saw all the lights.  The bar area is so beautiful with the Christmas lights and the Santa covered chairs.  They have an assortment of decorations for you to take pictures in front of.  Additionally, they have a variety of drinks you can order.  I ordered the Christmapolitan drink, but opted to get it without the alcohol.  They were able to accommodate that and make me a wonderful drink.  They also had some games you can play to pass the time and use up close to the 3 hours you paid for parking.

If you get the chance, please visit this pop up bar before they potentially move somewhere else!<//Text>

<Text>People often come up to me on the street & you know what they tell me?

"Hey Rodney, nice ass!"  No.

"Hey Rodney, how much?"  No.  Okay, sometimes.......;p

No, people say to me "Hey Rodney, why are you so happy?", to which I reply "I just got some hot tongue action, that's why!"

Senor Baja hit me debajo de cinturon, "below the belt", with the portion-size of their lengua burrito.
A hefty tongue burrito, with rice, beans, onions, cilantro and other goodies.  Only things missing were some guacamole & sour cream.  Otherwise, a fine filling meal for $5.99 plus tax.

Senor Baja is a closet Sauce Nazi, as they are stingy with their chili sauces.  They only give you 2 containers to put their chili in if you're ordering to-go.

Various specials are offered throughout the week, such as $1 fish tacos/Mon & Wed.

Ample booth seating, with banda music for your listening pleasure.  Parking is in private lots on both sides of the restaurant.  Senor Baja is an unpretentious, hole in the wall taqueria.  So, don't come in expecting ambiance for your first date.  You probably won't get a second one ;p

As for my lengua burrito, I enjoyed it.  The burrito was filling, didn't hurt the wallet and was a healthier choice than buying a McRib at McDonald's.  I'm purposefully avoiding it at all costs.  I used to love McRibs, but knowing all the unhealthy junk that's put in it, I'll pass.

I'll be back on a future Mon or Wed to try Senor Baja's famed fish tacos.  Also, their shrimp cocktail for $10+ definitely piqued my interest.

Recommend!< /Text><user_name>Rodney S</user_name>< resp>
None<//resp>

< Review>
People often come up to me on the street & you know what they tell me?

"Hey Rodney, nice ass!"  No.

"Hey Rodney, how much?"  No.  Okay, sometimes.......;p

No, people say to me "Hey Rodney, why are you so happy?", to which I reply "I just got some hot tongue action, that's why!"

Senor Baja hit me debajo de cinturon, "below the belt", with the portion-size of their lengua burrito.
A hefty tongue burrito, with rice, beans, onions, cilantro and other goodies.  Only things missing were some guacamole & sour cream.  Otherwise, a fine filling meal for $5.99 plus tax.

Senor Baja is a closet Sauce Nazi, as they are stingy with their chili sauces.  They only give you 2 containers to put their chili in if you're ordering to-go.

Various specials are offered throughout the week, such as $1 fish tacos/Mon & Wed.

Ample booth seating, with banda music for your listening pleasure.  Parking is in private lots on both sides of the restaurant.  Senor Baja is an unpretentious, hole in the wall taqueria.  So, don't come in expecting ambiance for your first date.  You probably won't get a second one ;p

As for my lengua burrito, I enjoyed it.  The burrito was filling, didn't hurt the wallet and was a healthier choice than buying a McRib at McDonald's.  I'm purposefully avoiding it at all costs.  I used to love McRibs, but knowing all the unhealthy junk that's put in it, I'll pass.

I'll be back on a future Mon or Wed to try Senor Baja's famed fish tacos.  Also, their shrimp cocktail for $10+ definitely piqued my interest.

Recommend!</Review>
